Transliteration used in this e-text:

« - a; ¬ - aa; þ - i; ® - ii; ¯ - u; ° -uu;
± - e; ²- ee; ³ - ai; ´ - o; µ- oo; ¶ - au.
ì - k; í - ng; î - c; ï - nj; ð - t; ñ - N; ò - th; ó - n-;
ô - p; õ - m; ö - y; ÷ - r; ø - l; ù - v; ú - z; û - L; ü - R; ý - n.

NOTE - II
There are two additional vowels in Finnish Language. They are two dots above "a" ("A") and
two dots above "o" ("O"). They are written in this e-text as a* (A*) and o* (O*) respectively.
